   - Has `note_candidates_on_method_error` which notes the candidates

3. `compiler/rustc_hir_typeck/src/method/mod.rs` - This file defines the `MethodError::Ambiguity` enum variant

Let me look more carefully at the specific functions that are most relevant to the ICE during trait method resolution.

The key functions are:
- `assemble_extension_candidates_for_trait` in probe.rs - collects candidates
- `assemble_extension_candidates_for_traits_in_scope` in probe.rs - collects candidates from in-scope traits
- `consider_candidates` in probe.rs - considers candidates and returns Ambiguity error
- `report_method_error` in suggest.rs - reports the ambiguous method error
- `note_candidates_on_method_error` in suggest.rs - notes the candidates in the error
